[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m709[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m736[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the current broken implementation with a safe stub that:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Validates expected block type** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mkeep lines [0m[1;36m722[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m726[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Validates stream has required data:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add stream length check similar to other handlers: [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mStream_CheckAndLogRequiredLengthWLog[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext->priv->log, s, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Reads and validates magic number** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mkeep lines [0m[1;36m728[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m733[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Handles remaining metadata safely:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the block contains additional metadata beyond the magic number, consume it [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby advancing the stream pointer without processing[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures the stream position is correct for subsequent blocks[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use: `[0m[1;35mStream_Seek[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;35mStream_GetRemainingLength[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` to skip any remaining [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Updates state machine:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add: `*pExpectedBlockType = WBT_FRAME_END;` to maintain proper state [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtransition[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Logs that metadata was skipped:**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add debug log: `[0m[1;35mWLog_Print[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext->priv->log, WLOG_DEBUG, [0m[32m"RFX_METADATA block[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mencountered and skipped"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Remove the dangerous write operation at line [0m[1;36m734[0m[39m**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Proper Implementation Details[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe corrected `rfx_process_message_metadata` function should:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Keep assertions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m716[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m720[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Keep expected block type validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m722[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m726[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Add stream length validation for at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmagic number[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Keep magic number read and validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m728[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m733[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Skip any remaining metadata bytes safely[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Update expectedBlockType to WBT_FRAME_END to maintain state machine[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Log the metadata block was processed[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Return TRUE[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis approach:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Eliminates the wild memory write vulnerability** by removing the global [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables and unsafe pointer operations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Maintains backward compatibility** by accepting WBT_METADATA blocks without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashing[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Preserves the state machine** by properly updating expectedDataBlockType[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Follows the safe pattern** used by other message handlers[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Doesn't break existing functionality** since no legitimate encoder produces [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata blocks[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Allows fuzzing to continue** testing other codec paths without triggering this [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Verification Points[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter implementing the fix:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The global variables `metadataBlock` and `metadataData` should be completely [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. No code should attempt to read optional metadata fields in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`rfx_process_message_frame_begin`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The `rfx_process_message_metadata` function should safely consume the block [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout memory operations[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The state machine should correctly transition from WBT_EXTENSION → WBT_METADATA [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ WBT_FRAME_END[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Fuzzing should not trigger SEGV on WBT_METADATA blocks[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Is Optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Root Cause:** Removes the dangerous global variables and pointer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marithmetic that cause the wild write[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes:** Only modifies the broken metadata handling code without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffecting other codec functionality[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Safe Fallback:** Treats metadata as optional/ignorable data that can be safely[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskipped[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Compatibility:** Accepts metadata blocks from external sources [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout crashing[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves State Machine:** Properly updates expectedDataBlockType to maintain [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol flow[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Data Loss:** Since no encoder writes metadata and no code uses it, skipping[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit has no functional impact[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. All other message processing functions remain unchanged[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The RFX codec continues to process frames, regions, tilesets normally[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The state machine for block ordering is preserved and corrected for metadata[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Stream processing continues correctly after metadata blocks[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Issues:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SEGV Crash:** Eliminated by removing the wild write operation and global [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Corruption:** Prevented by not performing any pointer arithmetic with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **State Machine:** Fixed by properly updating expectedDataBlockType[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Stability:** The fuzzer can now test metadata blocks without crashing[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects and Mitigation:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Metadata blocks are discarded:** This is acceptable since:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No encoder produces them[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No code consumes them[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The feature appears incomplete/experimental[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Future metadata support:** If needed, proper implementation would require:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding metadata fields to RFX_MESSAGE or RFX_CONTEXT structures[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reading and storing metadata from the stream[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using the metadata in rendering/processing[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This can be added later without affecting the fix[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe pattern of validating, reading, and skipping unknown/optional data is used [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the RFX codec:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `rfx_process_message_frame_begin` validates and reads only required fields[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other handlers skip optional fields by checking stream remaining length[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The main processing loop handles unknown blocks by returning FALSE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1329[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1332[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the same defensive programming approach while maintaining protocol[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompliance.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
